   <ul class="breadcrumb">

      <li><a href="<?php echo base_url();?>admin/content/agenda">Agenda</a> <span class="divider">/</span></li>
      <li class="active">Edit Konten</li>
   </ul>   

   <?php foreach ($var_agenda->result() as $agenda) {} ?>

   <div class="container-fluid">
      <div class="row-fluid">
        <?php if(isset($msg)) { ?>                        
              <div class="alert alert-error">
                <button type="button" class="close" data-dismiss="alert">×</button>

              </div>

            <input id="slug" type="text" value="<?php echo $agenda->slug;?>" name="slug" class="input-xlarge" />       
            
			<label>Tanggal Mulai</label>
			<div class="input-append date" id="dp1" data-date="<?php echo $agenda->tgl_mulai;?>" data-date-format="yyyy-mm-dd">
				<input class="span2" size="16" type="text" value="<?php echo $agenda->tgl_mulai;?>" name="tgl_mulai">
				<span class="add-on"><i class="icon-calendar"></i></span>
			</div>
			
			<label>Tanggal Selesai</label>
			<div class="input-append date" id="dp2" data-date="<?php echo $agenda->tgl_selesai;?>" data-date-format="yyyy-mm-dd">
				<input class="span2" size="16" type="text" value="<?php echo $agenda->tgl_selesai;?>" name="tgl_selesai">
				<span class="add-on"><i class="icon-calendar"></i></span>
			</div>
			
			<label>Jam</label>
            <input type="text" value="<?php echo $agenda->jam;?>" name="jam" class="input-xlarge" />       
			
			<label>Lokasi</label>
            <input type="text" value="<?php echo $agenda->lokasi;?>" name="lokasi" class="input-xlarge" />       
			
            <label>Konten</label>
            <textarea rows="3" name="content" class="input-xlarge"><?php echo $agenda->content;?></textarea>        
            <div class="form-actions">
              <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary">Save changes</button>
